###################################################
###   Country Adjectives / Adjectifs des pays   ###
###################################################
### Ex. "The [German] government decided..." => "Le gouvernement [allemand] a décidé de..." (singular masculine / masculin singulier)
defined_text = {
	name = GetAdjMS
	text = {
		trigger = { OR = { tag = AFG original_tag = AFG } }
		localization_key = FRLOC_AFG_ADJ_MS
	}

		trigger = { OR = { tag = ALB original_tag = ALB } }

				AND = { is_in_faction_with = JAP JAP = { is_faction_leader = yes } JAP = { has_completed_focus = JAP_west_pacific_treaty_organization } } # JAP_west_pacific_treaty_organization

				AND = { is_in_faction_with = SOV SOV = { is_faction_leader = yes } has_government = communism } # Comintern
				AND = { is_in_faction_with = GER GER = { is_faction_leader = yes } has_government = fascism } # Axis
			}
		}
		localization_key = FRLOC_E
	}

				AND = { is_in_faction_with = PRC PRC = { is_faction_leader = yes } SHX = { has_completed_focus = CHI_join_the_chinese_soviet } } # CHI_the_peoples_front/SHX-PRC

				AND = { is_in_faction_with = PRC PRC = { is_faction_leader = yes } XSM = { has_completed_focus = CHI_join_the_chinese_soviet } } # CHI_the_peoples_front/XSM-PRC
				AND = { is_in_faction_with = PRC is_in_faction_with = CHI OR = { PRC = { is_faction_leader = yes } CHI = { is_faction_leader = yes } } } # CHI_the_peoples_front (decision/event)
